           <h1>
            <a data-ga-content-type="article" data-linktype="headline" href="https://www.pennlive.com/sports/2021/03/updated-2021-piaa-boys-and-girls-basketball-championship-schedules.html">

            </a>
           </h1>
          </div>
          <div class="article__details">
           <div class="article__details--summary">
            Semifinal action takes place across the state on Monday and Tuesday. Hershey's Giant Center is the host venue for all 12 PIAA finals later in the week
